执行摘要Executive Summary

摘要Summary

StarBridge Portal（虚构样例）展示了一类多租户 SaaS 常见的组合风险：对象级授权缺失、Webhook 签名缺失、报表过滤拼接 SQL、链接预览 SSRF、导出下载路径遍历、批量赋值、支付回调伪造、前端 Token 存储、硬编码密钥、对象存储公开、CI 权限过大、数据库公网暴露以及 AI 成本滥用。该报告仅用于展示 Skill 的评分表、证据组织和多格式输出能力。StarBridge Portal (fictional example) demonstrates common multi-tenant SaaS risks: object-level authorization gaps, missing webhook signatures, SQL concatenation in report filters, link-preview SSRF, export path traversal, mass assignment, forged payment callbacks, frontend token storage, hardcoded keys, public object storage, excessive CI permissions, public database exposure, and AI cost abuse. The report is for demonstrating scorecard, evidence organization, and multi-format output only.

边界Boundary

授权：Authorization: [redacted]示例报告，不对应真实授权目标；所有系统名称、仓库地址、代码路径、端点、账号、证据和漏洞均为虚构。Example report only. It does not represent a real authorized target; all names, paths, endpoints, accounts, evidence, and findings are fictional.

范围：Scope: 公开示例报告：虚构 SaaS 协作平台，所有端点、文件路径、风险发现和测试证据均为演示内容。公开示例报告：虚构 SaaS 协作平台，所有端点、文件路径、风险发现和测试证据均为演示内容。

覆盖说明：Coverage Notes: 本报告用于演示格式，不可作为真实系统安全结论。若套用到真实项目，需要重新克隆/部署目标并重新填充证据。This report demonstrates the format only and must not be treated as a real security conclusion. A real target must be cloned/deployed and evidenced independently.

主动测试前置条件仅演示动态安全审查的低风险边界：临时依赖安装、临时数据库、loopback 服务、烟测、被动 DAST、响应头和 Cookie 检查。主动破坏性测试需要单独授权。
方法以此前真实项目安全审查报告的结构和版式为原型，但已将审查对象、漏洞类型、代码路径、端点、证据和整改建议全部替换为虚构内容，用于展示 yao-websecurity-skill 的报告交付形态。
覆盖台账示例台账覆盖 V001-V275 共 275 个检查项。虚构项目假设枚举 132 条路由，其中 API 44 条、后台 38 条、Webhook 6 条、导入导出 12 条；示例 SCA 和低级动态检查结果均为演示数据。

MethodologyThe layout is modeled after a prior real-project audit report, but the target, vulnerability set, code paths, endpoints, evidence, and remediation guidance have all been replaced with fictional content to demonstrate the report output.
Coverage LedgerThe example ledger covers V001-V275, 275 checks total. The fictional project assumes 132 routes, including 44 API routes, 38 admin routes, 6 webhook routes, and 12 import/export routes; SCA and low-risk dynamic results are demonstration data.

未检查项Not Checked Items

未检查项会降低覆盖率。若属于运行时或主动测试范围，需要补充授权、测试账号、部署 URL 或安全窗口。Not-checked items reduce coverage. Runtime or active-test items require authorization, test accounts, a deployed URL, or a safe test window.

没有未检查项。

残余风险与复测计划Residual Risk and Retest Plan

字段值
残余风险样例未覆盖真实运行时差异、真实云策略、真实对象存储 ACL、真实模型供应商策略和真实账号矩阵。
复测计划按 P0/P1 修复后，在隔离临时部署中复测授权矩阵、Webhook 签名、SQL 参数化、URL allowlist、导出路径沙箱、上传处理、CI 权限和 AI 配额控制。
FieldValue
Residual RiskThe example does not cover real runtime differences, cloud policies, object storage ACLs, model-provider policies, or account matrices.
Retest PlanAfter P0/P1 remediation, retest authorization matrices, webhook signatures, SQL parameterization, URL allowlists, export path sandboxing, upload handling, CI permissions, and AI quota controls in an isolated temporary deployment.
